### 7. High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Photograph Prompt

**Author**: [ケンイチ | AIスキルアカデミー『誰でもわかるAI活用術』](https://x.com/ChatgptAIskill)  **Date**: 2026-01-02  **Language**: en

> A highly detailed prompt designed to generate a sophisticated, high-end editorial photograph for a concept art magazine. It instructs the AI to invent a novel functional object based on a specified brand's aesthetic, emphasizing hyper-premium materials, cinematic studio lighting, and precise layout specifications for brand logo and product description text.

![High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Photograph Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508495498_1jfs1l_G9pi5wFaAAAV7WB.jpg)
![High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Photograph Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508495563_cebmbe_G9pi51cbQAAXAgF.jpg)
![High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Photograph Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508495836_wiqoa1_G9pi5wCaoAASRHh.jpg)
![High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Photograph Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508497484_0wzuyx_G9pi51Wb0AAPqts.jpg)

```
[BRAND NAME]: 
A high-end, glossy concept art magazine editorial photograph of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by the brand.

**1. The Concept & Object (AI Invention):**
Based on the design philosophy, heritage, and material vocabulary of the specified brand, the AI must invent a novel utility product (NOT standard clothing, shoes, or bags). Examples could be home goods, tech accessories, tools, or sporting equipment, reinterpretated through the brand's lens. The object should feel sculptural yet functional.

**2. Materials & Details (Hyper-Premium):**
The object is constructed from ultra-premium, highly tactile materials characteristic of the brand (e.g., patinated exotic leathers, brushed aerospace-grade titanium, sculpted matte ceramics, molded carbon fiber, or technical high-fashion textiles). Every detail is hyper-realistic: visible stitching, microscopic material grain, precision engravings, and complex texture contrasts.

**3. Photography & Lighting (Cinematic Studio):**
Shot on a medium format Phase One camera with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, with sharp focus on the hero details of the object and a creamy, smooth bokeh background. The lighting is sophisticated studio softbox lighting: gentle, enveloping fill light with precise rim lighting to accentuate contours and material textures.

**4. Environment:**
A seamless, impeccably clean studio cyclorama background in a pure, ultra-light pastel tone (e.g., desaturated mint, pale blush, or off-white), free of shadows.

**5. Layout & UI Elements (Strict Placement):**
- **Bottom Right Corner:** A small, understated, monochrome gray logo of the brand.
- **Bottom Left Corner:** Small, minimalist monochrome gray text describing the invented product. The font style looks like Manrope Regular with very tight tracking (kerning) and balanced line spacing. Example format: "CONCEPT STUDY: [AI inserts invented product name]. MATERIAL: [AI inserts main materials]. SS25."
```

[[Studio Lighting]]

### 8. 魅惑之美口红广告文案提示

**Author**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin)  **Date**: 2025-12-31  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超逼真的美妆广告图片，画面中一位女性倚靠在一支巨大的、光泽感十足的红色 MAC 唇膏旁，强调专业的影棚灯光、奢华的化妆品美学，并带有一个手写的“Devilish Beauty”文字元素。

![魅惑之美口红广告文案提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456159819_qs7un9_G9gQrljWIAACrUb.jpg)

```
A high-end, hyper-realistic beauty advertisement shot.

Composition:
Side-view composition of an attractive brunette woman, positioned slightly in profile. She is leaning her back confidently against a gigantic red lipstick, scaled dramatically larger than life. Her arms are crossed, posture strong and elegant, while she turns her head to look directly at the camera with a bold, self-assured expression.

Appearance:
She has smooth, luminous skin, deep brown hair styled sleek and polished, and striking red lipstick that perfectly matches the oversized product behind her. Her facial features are symmetrical and refined, with confident eyes and a subtle, knowing gaze.
She wears a minimalist black dress, form-fitting, elegant, and timeless.

Product:
The oversized lipstick is bright red, glossy, perfectly cylindrical, clearly branded {argument name="brand" default="MAC"} with realistic logo placement and premium material finish.

Text Element:
At the top of the image, the slogan “{argument name="slogan" default="Devilish Beauty"}” is written as if handwritten with red lipstick—bold, sensual strokes, slightly imperfect, glossy texture, natural lipstick smudge edges.

Background:
Pure white studio background, seamless, high-key, no visible shadows or distractions.

Lighting:
Professional studio lighting—soft key light on her face, gentle rim light to define her silhouette, subtle reflections on the lipstick tube. Clean, luxury cosmetic ad lighting.

Style & Quality:
Ultra-photorealistic, luxury fashion photography, crisp focus, natural skin texture, premium cosmetics campaign aesthetic, editorial magazine quality.

Negative Prompt; anime, illustration, CGI, cartoon, flat lighting, low detail, blurry, distorted anatomy, plastic skin, over-smoothed face, low-budget ad, cluttered background
```

### 12. 颜料管挤压：3D 浮雕星夜

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-29  **Language**: en

> 一个富有创意的提示模板，旨在分析一幅著名画作（如《星空》），并生成一张超现实的图像：一个巨大的油画颜料管被挤压到调色板上，挤出的颜料形成了被分析画作的 3D 景观，强调了粘稠的厚涂纹理和工作室照明效果。

![颜料管挤压：3D 浮雕星夜](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767166882317_0cdhnv_G9Oev9VXkAATyH0.jpg)
![颜料管挤压：3D 浮雕星夜](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767166882971_bu133f_G9Oev9XXoAAFOMT.jpg)

```
Do this for {argument name="painting name" default="Starry Night"}<instruction>

Input A is a Famous Painting (e.g., The Mona Lisa, The Scream). Analyze: The brushstroke technique, the 3D depth implied, and the hidden symbols. 
Goal: A "Paint Tube Squeeze." A giant, realistic oil paint tube sitting on a palette. 
Rules:
Action: The tube is being squeezed, and the paint coming out is not just a blob, but it forms the 3D landscape of the painting. The Mona Lisa's face is emerging in 3D relief from the 2D smear of paint. 
Texture: Viscous, thick oil paint texture (impasto). 
Props: Paintbrushes, a dirty rag, a palette knife, plus culture appropriate tools and environment and tiny 3D printed version of the painter on the desk drawing it on a tiny easel and a newspaper headline covering the inspiration behind it. 
Lighting: North-light studio lighting, true color representation. Output:
ONE image, 4:5, "artistic process" aesthetic. </instruction>
```

Apple Watch
Create a dynamic scene where the Apple Watch Ultra from Reference 1 breaks down into its individual components, with each piece leaving the dial in a controlled, forward-floating sequence that retains the original direction and perspective of the watch, maintaining the metallic finish, glass reflections, and rugged structure visible in the reference; place the detached orange strap behind the wrist while keeping the same soft, neutral studio lighting, the close-up composition of the arm, and the smooth muted background tone. Enhance micro-details, improve overall image fidelity, increase clarity, and make the colors more vibrant and saturated.

IPhone

### 21. 写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的综合性提示，旨在根据参考图像为 PVC 人偶生成一个超逼真的产品介绍布局。它包含了人偶设计的详细规格、构图（垂直 3:4 比例，包含主视觉和产品信息区域）、动作（静态姿势）、场景（中性摄影棚环境）、风格（超逼真渲染）、灯光（摄影棚灯光，带有光泽/哑光效果），以及产品名称、制造商、比例、价格、尺寸和材料的精确日文文本元素，包括多个突出不同特征的特写插图面板。

![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936084166_akbdxh_G8XTcGNaAAAmLN5.jpg)
![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936084050_etec6l_G8XTcGRaAAA3_TA.jpg)
![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936084588_wrkfsu_G8XTcGMbUAAghZN.jpg)
![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936086775_0ylrm3_G8XTcGOaoAALjeQ.jpg)

```
product_name: "{ARBITRARY_PRODUCT_NAME}"
manufacturer_name: "{ARBITRARY_MANUFACTURER_NAME}"

subject: >
  The character from reference image A, faithfully preserved in design, proportions,
  facial features, hairstyle, outfit details, and color palette.
  The character is transformed into a highly detailed, photorealistic PVC figure.
  Sculpting style and overall aesthetic are inferred directly from the reference image.
  The figure is presented as a 1/7 scale collectible.

composition: >
  Japanese-language product introduction layout inferred by the model.
  Vertical composition with a 3:4 aspect ratio.
  A large main visual of the full figure.
  A single, clearly defined product information area containing all textual elements.
  Product name logo and manufacturer name logo are each displayed exactly once.
  Multiple inset close-up panels are included.
  Each inset must focus on a different physical area or feature of the figure.
  No two inset panels may depict the same part or the same visual characteristic.
  Inset panels must be visually and conceptually distinct from one another.

action: >
  Static collectible figure pose with no movement.
  Emphasis on sculpt accuracy, proportions, and surface detail.

location: >
  Neutral studio-like environment inferred for product photography.
  Minimal, non-distracting background.

style: >
  Photorealistic product rendering and photography style.
  Artistic tone and mood inferred entirely from the reference image.

camera_lighting: >
  Camera angle and lighting inferred for clear presentation of a collectible figure.
  Realistic studio lighting interacting with PVC surfaces.
  Glossy highlights on hair and clothing.
  Matte finish on skin.
  Sharp focus with natural depth of field.
  Soft shadow beneath the figure as if placed on a flat surface.

colors: >
  Exact color reproduction based on the reference image.
  Background and graphic elements inferred to support readability of Japanese text.

text: >
  商品名：
  「{{product_name}}」
  ※ 商品名は必ず表示し、ロゴとして1箇所のみ表示する。

  メーカー名：
  「{{manufacturer_name}}」
  ※ メーカー名も必ず表示し、ロゴとして1箇所のみ表示する。

  スケール：
  1/7スケールフィギュア

  原型製作：
  {{manufacturer_name}}

  価格：
  フィギュアのスケール、造形密度、塗装表現から推論した
  販売価格を日本円で表示。

  サイズ：
  キャラクターの体型と1/7スケール設定から推論した
  全高をセンチメートル表記で表示。

  材質：
  フィギュアとして妥当な材

**Author**: [Chandan Singh](https://x.com/cbsingh_oo3)  **Date**: 2025-12-11  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张时尚、具有编辑风格的女性工作室肖像照。照片中，女性身着优雅飘逸的薄荷绿和鼠尾草绿长裙，裙摆处有戏剧性的高开衩。该提示词详细描述了服装、姿势、配饰（及膝绑带凉鞋）以及工作室灯光设置，以实现一张精致、杂志品质的全身照片。

![薄荷绿礼服中的时尚社论肖像 (JSON)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967726126_moo53u_G73K0EdaMAQ2GTi.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": "A stylish, high-fashion portrait of a woman seated, looking down at her flowing gown. The woman has long, wavy, dark brown hair with bangs, cascading over her shoulders. She is wearing an elegant, floor-length gown in varying shades of light mint and sage green. The bodice appears to be sleeveless or one-shouldered with a subtle, textured or patterned design (possibly white floral or abstract print). The skirt features a very high slit, dramatically revealing her legs. The fabric of the lower skirt is sheer and flowing chiffon, draped gracefully around the woman. She is wearing high-heeled **strappy sandals with straps extending all the way up to her thighs**, adorned with sparkling embellishments. One hand is gently holding the flowing fabric of the skirt. She is sitting on a small, rectangular object, possibly a red or dark orange ottoman or box, contrasting with the green. The backdrop is a seamless white photography paper or screen, partially visible as a roll on the floor. The setting is indoors, with hard, bright studio lighting that highlights the texture of the dress and the sheen on her skin. The mood is sophisticated, sensual, and editorial. Full body shot, high-resolution, magazine quality.",
  "style": [
    "high fashion editorial",
    "studio portrait",
    "glamour photography on ramp walk stage"
  ],
  "dominant_colors": [
    "mint green",
    "sage green",
    "white",
    "dark brown (hair)",
    "red/orange (seat)"
  ],
  "camera_settings": {
    "view": "full body/three-quarter shot",
    "lens": "85mm prime or similar (shallow depth of field suggested)",
    "lighting": "bright, professional studio lighting, strong highlight/shadow contrast"
  },
  "artist_inspiration": [
    "Vogue magazine spread",
    "fashion campaign imagery"
  ]
}

**Author**: [NanoInspire](https://x.com/NanoInspirate)  **Date**: 2025-12-09  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的商业时尚照片，内容是一位年轻女性身穿紧身红色连衣裙，头戴软呢帽，强调戏剧性的影棚灯光、高对比度以及性感、有力量的氛围。

![戏剧性红色时尚编辑肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440062777_tvgnrs_G7tuqrKXgAE5g9j.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_description": {
    "subject": "A sophisticated young woman, appearing to be in her early to mid-twenties, with a slender and curvaceous figure.",
    "face": "Full lips with a glossy, vibrant red lipstick, slightly parted. Defined eyebrows, sharp eyeliner creating a subtle cat-eye. Eyes are a piercing blue-gray, looking over her shoulder with a direct, alluring gaze. Skin is smooth with a dewy finish, showing subtle highlights on the cheekbones and cupid's bow.",
    "hair": "Dark brown hair, slicked back into a neat, low bun, emphasizing the facial structure and the hat.",
    "clothing": "A form-fitting, strapless red dress made of a ruched, stretch fabric that clings to the body. The ruching creates vertical textured lines across the dress, giving it a sculpted appearance. The neckline is a sweetheart or strapless bustier style, emphasizing the décolletage. Long, opera-length red gloves that reach past the elbows, made of a smooth, possibly satin or velvet-like material. The gloves are slightly gathered at the wrists and appear tight-fitting on the arms.",
    "accessories": "A wide-brimmed, structured red fedora hat positioned at a slight angle. Large, ornate gold earrings, possibly of an abstract or hammered metal design, visible beneath the hat. Red lipstick matching the dress and hat.",
    "environment": "A plain, dark gray studio backdrop, creating a strong contrast with the vibrant red of the subject's attire. The background is smooth and devoid of detail, ensuring the focus remains entirely on the subject.",
    "lighting": "Dramatic studio lighting. A key light positioned to the front-right of the subject, casting gentle shadows that define her form and the texture of the dress. A subtle fill light or bounce from the left to lift the shadows. Strong specular highlights on the lips, earrings, and potentially the fabric of the dress and gloves, indicating a polished surface. The lighting creates a sense of depth and highlights the contours of her body.",
    "atmosphere": "Sensual, elegant, powerful, and mysterious. The dominant red color evokes passion and confidence. The pose and lighting contribute to a feeling of allure and sophisticated drama."
  },
  "style": {
    "art_style": "Ultra-realistic commercial fashion photography, editorial style.",
    "color_grade": "Rich, saturated reds contrasted with deep grays. A slight contrast boost to enhance the dramatic feel, with skin tones remaining natural but luminous.",
    "texture_quality": "Extremely sharp focus on the subject, with incredible detail in fabric texture, skin pores (if visible), and makeup. High micro-contrast."
  },
  "camera_settings": {
    "camera": "Implied Medium Format or high-end full-frame sensor for exceptional detail.",
    "lens": "Likely a portrait lens, such as an 85mm or 105mm, to provide slight compression and flattering perspective. A lens with excellent sharpness and low distortion.",
    "aperture": "Wide open (e.g., f/1.4 or f/1.8) to ensure shallow depth of field and subject isolation."
  }
}

**Author**: [Vivek HY](https://x.com/Vivekhy)  **Date**: 2025-12-08  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成超细节的 8K 产品摄影，重点是精致的蕾丝内衣。它指定了场景（室内摄影棚，采用紫色/暖色调）、主体（女性手模手持产品），以及柔和的散射光、对蕾丝纹理的清晰对焦和 4:5 的纵向构图等技术细节，以实现干净、美观和专业的产品展示。

![8K 蕾丝内衣产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438576309_jfwvje_G7q1krFaMAAxXvF.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": {
    "scene": {
      "setting": "Indoor studio-style room with soft ambient lighting, purple and warm tones in the background. Modern sofa and minimal decor visible.",
      "mood": "Clean, aesthetic, professional product showcase atmosphere."
    },
    "subject": {
      "type": "female hand model",
      "pose": "Holding a pair of lace underwear stretched gently between both hands.",
      "details": "Only the arms and hands are visible, positioned in the foreground."
    },
    "product": {
      "type": "delicate lace underwear",
      "material": "Sheer floral lace with scalloped edges and soft {argument name="product color" default="white"} color.",
      "position": "Centered in the frame, held horizontally and fully visible.",
      "texture_details": "Fine lace patterns, transparency, embroidery and stitching clearly shown."
    },
    "composition": {
      "camera_angle": "Straight-on medium close-up shot focusing on the product.",
      "lighting": "Soft diffused lighting creating gentle highlights on the lace texture.",
      "background": "Blurred warm-toned studio environment with purple light accent.",
      "ratio": "4:5 portrait format."
    },
    "render_style": {
      "quality": "Ultra-detailed 8K product photography.",
      "tones": "Soft, clean, aesthetic, minimalistic.",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on lace underwear; background intentionally soft."
    }
  }
}

**Author**: [NanoInspire](https://x.com/NanoInspirate)  **Date**: 2025-12-08  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张身着泳衣的年轻女性的超写实商业/时尚摄影作品。它详细说明了拍摄对象的身体特征、服装（深海军蓝连体泳衣）、环境（灰泥墙），以及精密的相机设置（中画幅、85mm 镜头、f/2.8-f/4）和灯光，以营造一种性感、优雅和亲密的氛围。

![超逼真商业泳装摄影提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438567912_jirxao_G7qVxyTXMAAPVl3.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_description": {
    "subject": "A slender, young adult woman in her early 20s with an athletic build.",
    "face": "A captivating face with high cheekbones, a delicate jawline, and full lips. Her expression is alluring, with a subtle gaze over her shoulder. Her skin is smooth with visible pores and a healthy glow, with no prominent moles. Her eyes are a warm brown, and her gaze is directed slightly past the viewer.",
    "hair": "Long, wavy, dark brown hair that flows over her shoulders and back. The texture is soft and natural, with loose strands framing her face. It appears to be styled to look naturally voluminous.",
    "clothing": "A dark navy, form-fitting one-piece swimsuit. The neckline is a U-shape, sitting moderately low. The fabric is taut against her body, with no visible wrinkles or folds, indicating a snug fit. The leg openings are high-cut, emphasizing her hips and thighs. The fabric appears to have a slight sheen, typical of swimwear material.",
    "accessories": "A tiny stud earring in her left earlobe. Her fingernails are unpolished.",
    "environment": "An indoor setting with a textured, light beige wall. The wall has a slightly rough, stucco-like finish. Vertical shadows from an unseen window or blinds are cast diagonally across the wall and subtly onto the subject. The overall environment suggests a minimalist, studio-like space.",
    "lighting": "Soft, directional light source from the left, casting elongated, soft shadows on the wall. There are subtle specular highlights on her skin, particularly on her shoulder, arm, and thigh, indicating the direction of the light. The light is warm and emphasizes the texture of the wall and her skin.",
    "atmosphere": "The mood is sensual, elegant, and somewhat intimate. The lighting and pose create a feeling of relaxed confidence and natural beauty. The overall tone is warm and inviting."
  },
  "style": {
    "art_style": "Ultra-realistic commercial photography, editorial fashion",
    "color_grade": "Warm, sun-kissed tones with a focus on natural skin tones. The shadows have a slightly desaturated, cool undertone, providing a subtle contrast. The overall palette is dominated by warm beige, skin tones, and the deep navy of the swimsuit.",
    "texture_quality": "Extremely sharp focus on the subject's skin and hair, with incredible micro-contrast and detailed texture. A very subtle, fine grain may be present, mimicking high-quality photographic film. High level of realism."
  },
  "camera_settings": {
    "camera": "Medium Format",
    "lens": "85mm portrait lens, with slight compression to flatter the subject's form.",
    "aperture": "f/2.8 - f/4, creating a shallow depth of field and soft bokeh.",
    "iso": "Low ISO (e.g., 100-200) to ensure maximum detail and minimal noise.",
    "shutter_speed": "Fast shutter speed to freeze motion and ensure sharpness.",
    "white_balance": "Slightly warm white balance, around 5400K, to en"
}

### 33. Nano Banana Pro JSON 提示词：用于制作四格情绪拼贴画

**Author**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin)  **Date**: 2025-12-07  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro AI 工具设计的结构化 JSON 提示，用于生成一个四照片拼贴画。该拼贴画以超写实肖像摄影风格，通过特定的相机和灯光设置，展现了同一位女性主体在四种不同情绪下的状态——愤怒、沮丧、调情和开怀大笑。

![Nano Banana Pro JSON 提示词：用于制作四格情绪拼贴画](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421869907_nix231_G7khZjSWUAAoinG.jpg)

```
{
  "scene": {
    "format": "4_photo_collage",
    "layout": "2_columns_2_rows",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "label_position": "top_center_white_text",
    "background": "soft_minimal_studio_backdrop"
  },
  "subject": {
    "identity": "same_girl_from_reference",
    "appearance": {
      "hair": "{argument name="hair style" default="dark_brown_high_ponytail"}",
      "skin_tone": "{argument name="skin tone" default="warm_tan"}",
      "features": "same_face_structure",
      "accessories": ["{argument name="accessories" default="gold_hoop_earrings"}"],
      "outfit": "{argument name="outfit" default="bikini"}",
      "visible_area": "upper_body_chest_to_head",
      "makeup": "natural_glow"
    },

    "style": "hyper_realistic_portrait_photography",
    "camera": {
      "lens": "85mm_portrait",
      "framing": "upper_body_close_up",
      "lighting": "soft_diffused_beauty_light",
      "focus": "sharp_on_eyes_and_face"
    }

  },
  "photos": [
       { "mood": "{argument name="mood 1" default="ANGRY"}", "expression": "{argument name="expression 1" default="tense_brows_narrowed_eyes"}", "label": "Angry" },
   
    { "mood": "{argument name="mood 2" default="DEPRESSED"}", "expression": "{argument name="expression 2" default="downward_gaze_low_energy"}", "label": "Depressed" },

    { "mood": "{argument name="mood 3" default="FLIRTY"}", "expression": "{argument name="expression 3" default="half_smirk_head_tilt"}", "label": "Flirty" },

    { "mood": "{argument name="mood 4" default="LAUGHING"}", "expression": "{argument name="expression 4" default="open_mouth_genuine_laughter"}", "label": "Laughing" }

  ],

  "render_style": {

    "detail": "micro_skin_texture_hair_strands_realistic_shadows",

    "color_grade": "natural_skin_tones_high_dynamic_range"

  }

}

### 36. 超写实 Sabrina Carpenter 风格肖像

**Author**: [LexiPrompt](https://x.com/Artist04048661)  **Date**: 2026-03-30  **Language**: en

> 一份为 Nano Banana Pro 模型设计的详细 JSON 提示词，旨在生成一张超写实的 RAW 格式影棚肖像，呈现出具有柔和高定、复古 Coquette 风格的 Sabrina Carpenter 形象。主体呈跪姿，身穿粉色缎面紧身胸衣和白色歌剧手套，背景为带有气球的柔和粉色调。

![超写实 Sabrina Carpenter 风格肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774939646059_4wtu4z_HEqhjvzWMAADouZ.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {

> 一个图生图提示词，旨在对现有工作室肖像中的面部和发型进行精确替换。它要求在保持原始身体、姿势、服装、光线（柔和、漫射）和背景（纯深红色）不变的同时，无缝整合来自参考图像的新面部和头发，确保达到照片级的真实感。

![影棚肖像照的换脸和发型功能](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804241083_l1flc9_G-9UEm8XQAEvLx0.jpg)

```
{
  "Ultra-realistic studio portrait of a young woman in a three-quarter profile pose, head slightly turned toward the camera. She is wearing a black textured blazer over a dark top with minimal accessories, including a small hoop earring. Background is a solid deep red studio backdrop with a smooth gradient. Lighting is soft, diffused studio lighting with gentle shadows and even skin tones. Replace ONLY the face and hairstyle using the reference image. Keep body, pose, clothing, background, lighting, camera angle, framing, and image quality exactly the same. Ensure the new face matches the original head size, angle, and expression with seamless skin blending and natural hair integration. Photorealistic, cinematic quality, sharp focus on eyes, shallow depth of field.",
  "negative_prompt": "face distortion, wrong head size, mismatched skin tone, altered pose, changed clothing, different background, lighting mismatch, blurry face, artifacts, unrealistic hair, over-smoothing",
  "style": "photorealistic",
  "camera": {
    "shot": "close-up portrait",
    "angle": "three-quarter view",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow"
  },
  "lighting": "soft studio lighting",
  "background": "solid deep red",
  "quality": "high resolution",
  "face_swap": {
    "enabled": true,
    "change_only": ["face", "hairstyle"],
    "preserve": ["pose", "body", "clothing", "background", "lighting", "camera_angle"]
  }
}

      "tattoos": "Stylized black swirl tattoos visible on her shoulder"
    },

      "bottom_left": "Confident pose with arms crossed, smiling at the camera",
      "bottom_right": "Candid laughter with hair blowing mid-air"

### 81. 电商工作室肖像与 UI 叠加

**Author**: [ΛRMIN | AI](https://x.com/Arminn_Ai)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多层提示，旨在生成一张高对比度、三维的影棚肖像，并叠加模拟的手机浏览器界面。它指定使用体积感影棚照明，使主体在平面背景上清晰突出，并有四个倾斜、重叠的白色浏览器窗口将图像分割，非常适合概念性电商或数字艺术。

![电商工作室肖像与 UI 叠加](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682069943_afvdcj_G96-CQsWQAAn4_k.jpg)
![电商工作室肖像与 UI 叠加](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682070043_ic8pmg_G96-Cg3WsAANGwl.jpg)

```
Subject Reference: A full-body portrait of [INSERT SUBJECT NAME].
Scene Description: A full-body, centered portrait of the subject [INSERT POSE DESCRIPTION]. The subject has [INSERT EXPRESSION], staring directly at the camera. The immediate background behind the subject is a [INSERT BACKGROUND TYPE, e.g., seamless, pure high-key white studio backdrop]. Crucially, the subject is lit with volumetric studio lighting that creates deep definitions, realistic shadows, and a strong 3D quality on her body and the folds of the outfit, distinguishing her sharply from the flat background without casting shadows on the floor.

CRITICAL DETAIL (UI Layer): The entire photographic image is digitally layered beneath a simulated mobile phone browser interface overlay. Four distinct, clean, white, rectangular browser window elements are stacked vertically and angled slightly, segmenting the subject. Each window bar contains the sharp text '[INSERT LINK OR TEXT HERE]'. ### 99. Nano Banana Pro 的 9 宫格编辑照片网格提示

**Author**: [Pawan | AI Tech Girl](https://x.com/AITechGirl)  **Date**: 2025-12-07  **Language**: en

> 这是一个详细的多镜头提示，旨在“Nano Banana Pro”风格下，在干净、柔和的米色影棚环境中生成 3x3 的编辑照片网格。它详细说明了九个不同肖像镜头的角色外观、灯光、构图、相机设置（镜头、光圈、景深）和整体氛围，重点在于亲密、内省和以角色为主导的编辑极简主义。

![Nano Banana Pro 的 9 宫格编辑照片网格提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421886891_qpc6ze_G7lw2p6aIAAwTxV.jpg)

```
Editorial 3x3 photo grid in a clean soft beige studio. 
Character (matches reference 100%) wearing lightweight dark navy shirt, ivory trousers, barefoot for raw simplicity. 
Lighting: large diffused key light directly front-right, silver reflector left, subtle rim from top. 
Shots to include: 1. extreme close-up of lips + cheekbone with blurred hand partially covering (85mm, f/1.8, razor-thin DOF); 
2. tight crop on eyes looking into lens with reflection of light strip visible (85mm, f/2.0); 
3. black & white close portrait resting chin on fist, face filling frame (50mm, f/2.2); 
4. over-shoulder shot, blurred foreground fabric curtain framing half face (85mm, f/2.0); 
5. very close frontal with hands overlapping face, light streak across eyes (50mm, f/2.5); 
6. tight angled portrait showing hair falling into eyes, soft-focus background (85mm, f/2.2); 
7. crop of hands touching jawline, eyes cropped out (50mm, f/3.2, detail-focused); 
8. half-body seated sideways on low cube, head turned sharply away, blurred foreground (35mm, f/ 4.5); 
9. intense close-up of profile with single tear-like water droplet, cinematic light slice across (85mm, f/ 1.9). 
Angles: mostly tight headshots with slight high/low tilts, maintaining variation. Capture RAW, professional muted grade, smooth tonal contrast, subtle cinematic grain. Mood: intimate, introspective, character-led editorial minimalism with delicate use of fabric as prop.
```

### 105. 风格化 3D 角色渲染（极简卡通）的 JSON 提示

**Author**: [Arce.](https://x.com/arceyul)  **Date**: 2026-02-05  **Language**: en

![风格化 3D 角色渲染（极简卡通）的 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770359944942_ao3rp2_HAY1HiWXwAAN2CM.jpg)
![风格化 3D 角色渲染（极简卡通）的 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770359945027_aib1sm_HAY1HflWQAA5G5q.jpg)
![风格化 3D 角色渲染（极简卡通）的 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770359945165_7cx15j_HAY1HfIX0AAfCLl.jpg)
![风格化 3D 角色渲染（极简卡通）的 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770359945665_3v7t64_HAY1HfJWMAAi6jH.jpg)

```
{
 "task": "image_style_transfer_3d_character",
 "input": {
 "source_image": "USER_UPLOADED_IMAGE",
 "preserve_identity": true,
 "preserve_pose": true,
 "preserve_composition": true
 },
 "style_reference": {
 "render_style": "stylized_3d_character",
 "aesthetic": "soft_minimal_cartoon_3d",
 "inspiration": [
 "pixar_like_but_more_minimal",
 "toy_figure_render",
 "clean_product_character_design"
 ]
 },
 "character_design": {
 "skin": {
 "material": "smooth_matte_plastic",
 "texture": "soft_uniform",
 "subsurface_scattering": "gentle"
 },
 "facial_features": {
 "eyes": "half_closed_bored_expression",
 "eyelids": "heavy",
 "nose": "rounded_simplified",
 "mouth": "flat_neutral",
 "ears": "simplified_rounded"
 },
 "emotion": "unimpressed_calm_bored"
 },
 "clothing": {
 "style": "minimal_streetwear",
 "details": "no_logos_no_patterns",
 "fabric": "soft_matte"
 },
 "accessories": {
 "headwear": "simple_baseball_cap_optional",
 "ear_accessories": "wireless_earbuds_optional"
 },
 "lighting": {
 "setup": "studio_softbox",
 "shadows": "very_soft",
 "contrast": "low",
 "highlights": "subtle"
 },
 "background": {
 "type": "solid_color",
 "color_palette": [
 "muted_green",
 "pastel_tone"
 ],
 "gradient": "none"
 },
 "camera": {
 "angle": "front_facing",
 "framing": "medium_close_up",
 "lens": "50mm_equivalent",
 "distortion": "none"
 },
 "render_quality": {
 "resolution": "high",
 "edges": "clean",
 "noise": "none",
 "realism_balance": "stylized_over_realistic"
 },
 "output": {
 "consistency": "high",
 "style_strength": "strong",
 "photorealism": false
 }
}
```

### 114. 2000 年代初期视频游戏渲染风格迁移

**Author**: [fofr](https://x.com/fofrAI)  **Date**: 2026-01-19  **Language**: en

> 一个文本提示，旨在将给定图像转换为 2000 年代早期视频游戏的渲染美学，特别是模仿 Maya 4.0 渲染的外观。它侧重于低多边形几何体、低分辨率纹理和雾化远距离物体等大气效果，同时明确避免像素艺术或体素风格。

![2000 年代初期视频游戏渲染风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890735407_gwm2z0_G_B_Z9fXAAAZLep.jpg)
![2000 年代初期视频游戏渲染风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890735785_lglk0f_G_B_hMaW8AAjgyt.jpg)

```
Low poly, low res textures
- Distant objects get simplified and fogged out
- Avoids gotchas like pixel art and voxels
- Based on Maya 4.0 rendering
```

[[Style Transfer]]

### 115. 高端街头摄影改造

**Author**: [Harboriis](https://x.com/harboriis)  **Date**: 2026-01-19  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的指令提示，用于将上传的参考图像转换为旅行者/摄影师的高端街头摄影肖像。它要求保留姿势和构图，同时增强服装纹理，应用带有暖色边缘光的电影级冷色调分级，并模拟浅景深定焦镜头效果。

![高端街头摄影改造](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890649998_sozw27_G_BPm1FWIAAGZbR.jpg)

```
transform the photo a reference image into a high-end street-photography portrait of a traveler/photographer leaning casually on a lamp post in front of a historic tower. Keep the original pose and composition: standing with left leg bent and foot on the lamp base, right leg relaxed, left hand in jacket pocket, right hand holding a camera down by the thigh, shoulders slightly turned to camera, chin up and gaze off-frame. Preserve the camera, and textured jacket but enhance and stylize as follows:

Wardrobe & accessories: keep the dark parka/jacket but enrich fabric texture (subtle waxed canvas look), change inner hoodie to a soft charcoal knit, keep blue jeans but slightly deepened to rich indigo with natural creasing. Emphasize the high-top sneakers boost contrast on black-and-white panels and add faint scuff details for

realism. Add a small messenger bag strap across the chest and a compact leather wrist strap on the camera. Lighting & color: cinematic cool-tone grade (soft blue shadows) with warm golden rim light hitting the left side of the face and shoulder (suggest late-afternoon sun). Slightly boost contrast and midtones to create punch without losing skin detail. Add subtle film grain and gentle vignette to focus on the subject.

Camera & optics: emulate 35mm-50mm prime look, shallow DOF (f/1.8-2.8) so the tower and crowd become painterly bokeh while the subject remains razor-sharp. Slight perspective correction to emphasize the tower peek. behind his shoulder. Enhance catchlight/reflection in the eyes (or sunglasses reflection if present) and sharpen

camera details.

Background & atmosphere: keep the busy pedestrian scene but soften and desaturate it so the subject pops; raise clarity and texture on the stone tower so it reads as a strong architectural anchor. Add a few falling autumn leaves and a faint wet-pavement sheen to suggest recent rain (subtle reflections under shoes).. Final touches: natural skin retouching (preserve stubble and pores), boost micro-contrast on jacket and jeans,

accentuate lens/glass reflections on the camera. Export as photorealistic, vertical 4K editorial crop with high

detail.

Position (short): standing, left foot on lamp base, leaning against lamppost, camera in right hand, left hand in pocket, gaze off-frame.
```

[[Style Transfer]] [[Street Photography]] [[Cinematic Color Grading]] [[Bokeh Effect]]

### 121. 2D 到 3D 到 VRM 到插画工作流程

**Author**: [Alone1M](https://x.com/Alone1Moon)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: ja

> 一个复杂的多步骤工作流程，首先在 Nano Banana Pro 中使用 2D 参考图像（两视图绘图），将其转换为 3D 模型，然后是 VRM，摆好姿势，截取屏幕截图，最后再次使用 Nano Banana Pro 将屏幕截图转换为插画风格。

![2D 到 3D 到 VRM 到插画工作流程](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682246467_sqjcx8_G957WoZa0AAoBQS.jpg)

![2D 到 3D 到 VRM 到插画工作流程](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682248118_jybq9f_G957l9EaAAA8j4C.jpg)

```
Nano Banana Proの{argument name="参照画像" default="二面図画像"}から、3Dモデルを作成し、それをVRMに変換。ツールでポーズを付けてスクショ。そのスクショを元に{argument name="最終スタイル" default="イラストスタイル"}にNano Banana Proで再び変換。
```

### 124. 粉彩插画风格迁移（需提供参考图）

**Author**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u)  **Date**: 2026-01-04  **Language**: en

> 一个 JSON 提示，用于根据上传的图片（仅用于身份/肖像）生成手绘粉彩铅笔插画，改变姿势并将主体置于开放的粉彩公园环境中，营造清新、愉悦的氛围。

![粉彩插画风格迁移（需提供参考图）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767607063118_de4osl_G9yyyA9agAAtFiE.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": "Use the uploaded image strictly as an identity reference (face and likeness only). Change the pose to a relaxed side-profile stance with the subject slightly turned, one shoulder forward and head gently tilted, giving a candid feel. Place the subject in a new background: an open pastel park setting with soft clouds, light greenery, and simple abstract shapes. Render the scene in a hand-drawn pastel illustration style with clean but slightly rough pencil outlines, visible strokes, and gentle shading. Use bright yet natural pastel colors with warm tones. Facial features remain simple and cute with dot eyes and a small calm smile. Keep the overall mood light, friendly, and fresh.",
  "style": "hand-drawn pastel pencil illustration",
  "lighting": "soft daylight",
  "color_palette": "bright natural pastels",
  "texture": "visible pencil strokes, soft shading",
  "face_style": "simple features, dot eyes, small smile",
  "proportions": "semi-cartoon realistic",
  "mood": "fresh, relaxed, cheerful",
  "background": "pastel park scene with minimal clouds and greenery"
}

### 131. 保持身份的故事书插画

**Author**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u)  **Date**: 2025-12-30  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的提示，用于将上传图片中的主体转换为温暖、愉快的绘本插画风格，使用彩色铅笔和柔和的水彩晕染效果，严格保留主体的身份、面部结构和相似度，同时采用可爱、半卡通的风格。

![保持身份的故事书插画](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454955920_vkhzqq_G9cdJOwacAAO-Kp.jpg)
![保持身份的故事书插画](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454956230_vkciej_G9cdJQJaYAIgksE.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": "Use the uploaded image strictly as the identity and pose reference. Preserve the same person, facial structure, hairstyle, age, gender, body proportions, and overall likeness without adding or removing any person. Do not alter identity. Transform the subject into a hand-drawn storybook-style illustration created with colored pencils and soft watercolor washes.\n\nIllustration Style:\nHand-drawn colored pencil illustration with clean, confident line art and slightly rough, organic pencil outlines. Pencil strokes should be clearly visible and layered, giving a natural hand-drawn feel. Combine this with gentle watercolor wash textures that softly blend colors without overpowering the pencil lines.\n\nColor & Texture:\nUse bright pastel colors with lighter, cheerful, and vivid tones while keeping natural saturation. Colors should feel soft and cozy, never harsh or neon. Apply flat yet detailed coloring with subtle watercolor gradients. Minimal shadows, soft highlights only, no dramatic lighting. No realism, no photo texture, no hyper-detail.\n\nFacial Features & Expression:\nSimplified, cute facial features in a semi-cartoon realistic proportion. Dot-style eyes, small gentle smiles, soft rounded face shapes. Expressions should feel warm, friendly, innocent, and approachable. Keep facial details minimal but expressive.\n\nMood & Atmosphere:\nWarm, cozy, and cheerful atmosphere with a wholesome children’s book illustration feel. Friendly and comforting tone, suitable for a storybook or picture book. The overall mood should feel calm, joyful, and inviting.\n\nRendering Rules:\nHigh clarity illustration, clean edges, no blur. No photographic realism, no cinematic lighting, no 3D render, no digital painting look. Avoid heavy shading, deep shadows, glossy skin, or realistic textures.\n\nBackground:\nSimple, soft, illustrated background that complements the subject without distraction. Use pastel colors, gentle shapes, and minimal detail to maintain a storybook aesthetic.\n\nFinal Output:\nA cozy, cheerful, hand-illustrated children’s book style artwork with colored pencil linework and soft watercolor textures, maintaining exact identity from the uploaded image while transforming it into a warm, friendly, semi-cartoon illustration.",
  "negative_prompt": "photorealism, hyper-realistic, realistic skin texture, photo texture, cinematic lighting, dramatic shadows, dark tones, neon colors, glossy skin, 3D render, oil painting, digital painting, anime style, manga style, vector art, pixel art, blur, noise, grain, extra people, face change, identity change, exaggerated realism",
  "quality": "high",
  "clarity": "very high",
  "style_strength": "strong illustration style",
  "reference_usage": "face and identity preservation required"
}
```

[[Style Transfer]]

### 140. Obsidian Kintsugi 自动机风格迁移提示词

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-24  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂风格迁移提示，指示 AI 将输入照片（输入 A）转换为“黑曜石金缮自动机”状态。这种转换要求在保留精确姿势和几何结构的同时，使用抛光黑曜石、陈旧象牙、发条机械装置和发光的金色金缮裂纹来重建所有表面，并以戏剧性的高对比度照明进行渲染。

![Obsidian Kintsugi 自动机风格迁移提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935950052_i2epyo_G80kPLAXQAAGGtW.jpg)
![Obsidian Kintsugi 自动机风格迁移提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935949688_7mz1zp_G80jZ9mXUAA21iT.jpg)

```
<instruction>
Input A is the subject photo. Preserve exact pose and scene geometry.

Goal: Transform Input A into a 'Obsidian Kintsugi Automaton' state.
Rules:
 - Spatial Fidelity: Preserve every character's exact silhouette using 'Obsidian Kintsugi Automaton' Reconstruction engine
 - Materiality: All surfaces are reconstructed as Polished Obsidian and Aged Ivory with Clockwork Automaton and Kintsugi Ceramic architecture.
 - Technical Spec: Advanced Houdini/Blender simulation logic. Internal gears turn within the obsidian, and golden light pulses through the Kintsugi cracks.
 - Lighting: Dramatic, high-contrast lighting highlighting the reflective obsidian and glowing gold.
 - Rendering: Photorealistic, 4K, macro-detail focus.

Output: ONE image, high-fidelity transformation.
</instruction>
```

[[Style Transfer]]

### 141. 羊毛纱线缠绕艺术风格迁移提示词

**Author**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u)  **Date**: 2025-12-24  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的结构化提示词，指示 AI 将用户上传的参考图像转换为“毛线缠绕艺术”风格。该提示词详细说明了材料、技术（粗毛线、可见线圈）和渲染设置，以实现一种手工制作的、冬季工艺品美学，且不包含任何线条艺术或绘画元素。

![羊毛纱线缠绕艺术风格迁移提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935938033_fef72c_G85dp-fagAY7Go_.jpg)

{
  "reference_image": "UPLOAD_USER_IMAGE_HERE",
  "art_style": {
    "type": "wool_yarn_wrap_art",
    "technique": "thick_yarn_wrapped_shapes",
    "handmade_winter_craft": true,
    "no_line_art": true,
    "no_drawing": true,
    "no_paint": true
  },

    "material": "soft_wool_yarn",

    "wrap_style": "visible_looped_and_wrapped_threads",
    "direction": "natural_hand_wrapped_flow",
    "imperfection": "handmade_variation"
  },
  "subject": {
    "style": "cute_yarn_doll_look",
    "pose": "simple_gentle_pose",
    "expression": "soft_and_sweet"
  },
  "color_style": {
    "look": "natural_wool_colors",
    "finish": "matte_soft",
    "no_gloss": true
  },
  "background": {
    "type": "fabric_or_cardboard_base",
    "texture": "subtle_craft_surface"
  },
  "render_settings": {
    "resolution": "4K",
    "quality": "ultra_high",

    "winter_handmade_feel": true
  },

    "line_art",
    "embroidery_stitch",
    "felt_applique",

### 142. 毛毡布贴花艺术风格转换提示词

**Author**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u)  **Date**: 2025-12-24  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的结构化提示，指示 AI 将用户上传的参考图像转换为“毛毡布贴艺术”风格。该提示明确指定了材料（柔软羊毛毛毡）、可见缝线（毯边缝/平针缝）以及可爱、手工制作的毛毡娃娃外观，并明确排除了数字插图或照片级真实感渲染。

![毛毡布贴花艺术风格转换提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935946368_duagvk_G85cYJgagAAQFCv.jpg)
![毛毡布贴花艺术风格转换提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935949260_i25dn6_G85cYJRacAAOvXj.jpg)

```
{
  "reference_image": "UPLOAD_USER_IMAGE_HERE",
  "art_style": {
    "type": "felt_fabric_applique_art",
    "technique": "cut_fabric_shapes_stitched_together",
    "handmade_winter_craft": true,
    "no_line_art": true,
    "no_drawing": true,
    "no_painting": true
  },
  "fabric_details": {
    "material": "soft_wool_felt",
    "fabric_thickness": "slightly_thick_winter_felt",
    "edges": "clearly_cut_fabric_edges",
    "stitch_type": [
      "blanket_stitch",
      "running_stitch"
    ],
    "thread_visibility": "visible_contrast_thread"
  },
  "subject": {
    "style": "cute_handmade_felt_doll",
    "pose": "simple_static_pose",
    "expression": "sweet_and_gentle"
  },
  "color_style": {
    "look": "muted_winter_felt_colors",
    "finish": "soft_matte",
    "no_shine": true
  },
  "background": {
    "type": "plain_felt_or_cotton_base",
    "texture": "soft_fabric_surface"
  },
  "render_settings": {
    "resolution": "4K",
    "quality": "ultra_high",
    "craft_texture_priority": true,
    "handmade_feel": true
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "line_art",
    "embroidery_fill",
    "digital_illustration",
    "photo_realistic",
    "painting",
    "vector",
    "smooth_ai_texture",
    "plastic_look"
  ]
}
```

### 143. 手绣线艺术风格迁移提示

**Author**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u)  **Date**: 2025-12-24  **Language**: en

> 这是一个针对 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 的结构化提示，指示 AI 将用户上传的参考图像转换为“手绣线艺术”风格。该提示明确指定了材料（黄麻/粗麻布上的棉线）、可见的针脚线和可爱的、手工制作的玩偶外观，并明确排除了线条艺术、绘画或数字插画。

![手绣线艺术风格迁移提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935945353_4ghb73_G85X-qdagAA9Irs.jpg)

```
{
  "reference_image": "UPLOAD_USER_IMAGE_HERE",
  "identity_preservation": {
    "face_similarity": "high",
    "exact_likeness": true
  },
  "art_style": {
    "type": "hand_embroidery_thread_art",
    "technique": "fabric_stitch_illustration",
    "material_look": "colored_threads_on_cloth",
    "no_line_art": true,
    "no_paint": true,
    "no_digital_brush": true
  },
  "fabric_details": {
    "base_fabric": "jute_burlap_cotton_texture",
    "thread_type": "cotton_embroidery_thread",
    "stitch_visibility": "clearly_visible_thread_lines",
    "fill_style": "dense_thread_filling",
    "edges": "stitched_outlines_not_drawn"
  },
  "subject": {
    "style": "cute_handcrafted_doll_look",
    "expression": "soft_gentle",
    "pose": "simple_childlike_pose"
  },
  "color_style": {
    "look": "thread_color_natural_tones",
    "finish": "matte_fabric_finish",
    "no_gloss": true
  },
  "background": {
    "type": "plain_fabric_surface",
    "texture": "woven_cloth_visible"
  },
  "render_settings": {
    "quality": "ultra_high",
    "resolution": "4K",
    "handmade_feel": true,
    "craft_art_priority": true
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "line_art",
    "pencil",
    "sketch",
    "digital_illustration",
    "painting",
    "photo_realistic",
    "smooth_ai",
    "plastic_texture",
    "vector_style"
  ]

### 149. 图像转绘画复刻提示词

**Author**: [うみつる](https://x.com/umitsuru_fire)  **Date**: 2025-12-14  **Language**: ja

> 一份详细的提示，指示 Nano Banana Pro 复制一张所附的女性图片，使用特定的艺术技巧，最终呈现出一种模拟油画风格，带有动漫般的线条艺术基础、厚重的颜料阴影和花园背景。最终输出应包括原图中的女性自豪地展示这幅生成的画作。

![图像转绘画复刻提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991362272_ff6t4t_G8ITEi6bEAA9VF7.jpg)
![图像转绘画复刻提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991362285_9yxj6k_G8ITEi5aQAE7YXR.jpg)

```
添付の女性を下記の技法で再現して。
壁に掛かったアナログの油絵。全体的に淡い色で。背景は女性にあった草木が咲いた庭。

塗り: アニメ調の線画をベースにしつつ、影やハイライトの入れ方は絵画的（厚塗り風）です。特に髪の毛の束感や、シャツのシワの陰影が丁寧に描かれています。

その絵の前で、実写の画像の女性が嬉しそうに絵を紹介している。
縦横比{argument name="縦横比" default="9:16"}
```

[[Style Transfer]] [[Oil Painting]]

### 150. Ink Drawing Style Transfer Prompt

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2025-12-14  **Language**: zh

> A prompt template designed to transform an uploaded image into a detailed ink drawing style, specifically using cross-hatching and fine line work (micron pen sketchbook style) with high contrast black ink on textured white paper, while isolating the main subject and removing the background.

![Ink Drawing Style Transfer Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991386142_dg66d5_G8Hw0NQbMAAvy92.jpg)
![Ink Drawing Style Transfer Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991386247_8xg3l8_G8Hw0NSaMAEKpjQ.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_template": "A detailed ink drawing based on {argument name="image reference" default="[insert image reference here]"}, isolating the main subject. Rendered in a traditional micron pen sketchbook style. Shading, texture, and patterns are achieved exclusively through dense cross-hatching and fine line work, using high contrast black ink on textured white paper. The subject is centered with vast negative space, completely removing the original photo's background."
}
```

### 153. 图像转换为极简矢量海报

**Author**: [Yapper](https://x.com/yapper_so)  **Date**: 2025-12-11  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂、结构化提示，旨在将现有图像转换为简洁、极简主义的矢量风格海报。它要求进行几何简化，使用受限的调色板（3–6 种颜色，无渐变），采用平面照明，并保留基本特征，同时去除所有照片级真实感细节和纹理。此提示需要输入图像进行转换。

![图像转换为极简矢量海报](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967671182_e5chfe_G76855lW4AIyWq7.jpg)
![图像转换为极简矢量海报](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967671276_9tw8p0_G76855lWwAAsVft.jpg)
![图像转换为极简矢量海报](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967671365_2s7xj8_G76855vWgAA-tYI.jpg)
![图像转换为极简矢量海报](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967673323_m2lhjk_G7686-6XYAA56oH.jpg)

```
{ "task": "Transform the provided image into a minimal vector-style poster.", "style": { "overall_look": "Flat-design, geometric simplification, minimalist vector art", "color_palette": { "type": "restricted", "description": "Use a reduced palette of 3–6 harmonious colors with clean tonal separation and no gradients.", "constraints": [ "No photorealistic rendering", "No texture or noise", "Avoid excessive detail" ] }, "shapes": { "treatment": "Reduce all forms to essential geometric contours and solid shapes.", "linework": "Use clean, even-weight line art or optionally no outlines depending on poster coherence.", "abstraction_level": "High, but not so high that the subject becomes unrecognizable." }, "lighting": { "handling": "Remove realistic lighting. Replace shadows and highlights with simplified, flat blocks of color or omit them entirely.", "allowed_effects": ["Hard-edge shadow shapes", "Subtle tonal areas"], "forbidden_effects": ["Soft shadows", "Complex reflections", "Photographic highlights"] } }, "subject_preservation": { "identity": "Maintain recognizable identity through silhouette, proportions, key facial landmarks, and essential features.", "proportions": "Keep accurate relative scale of body, head, and major elements.", "essential_details": [ "Define only the most important features needed for recognition.", "Remove fine texture, hair strands, pores, and small clothing details." ] }, "composition": { "framing": "Match the original crop unless specified otherwise.", "background": { "treatment": "Simplify into 1–2 large flat color fields or abstract geometric forms.", "forbidden_details": ["Real textures", "Complex scenery", "Photographic depth of field"] }, "hierarchy": "Subject should remain the focal point, with background serving as supportive minimal structure." }, "color_and_balance": { "poster_aesthetic": "High clarity, bold contrast, and legible silhouette.", "white_balance": "Neutral; avoid warm or cool photographic shifts.", "edge_integrity": "All edges must be crisp, clean, and consistently stylized." }, "output_requirements": { "format": "Flat, poster-like vector appearance (though raster output is acceptable).", "resolution": "Match original image resolution unless otherwise instructed.", "consistency": "No added text, logos, watermarks, or elements not present in the original." }, "prohibited_changes": [ "Do not alter identity.", "Do not add new objects or remove essential ones.", "No stylization that contradicts minimal vector aesthetics (e.g., painterly strokes, gradients, 3D shading)." ], "goal_summary": "Create a clean, minimalist vector-style interpretation of the original image, preserving silhouette, proportions, and essential identity while removing all non-essential details and realistic lighting cues." }
```

[[Style Transfer]] [[Poster Design]] [[Flat Design]] [[Limited Color Palette]]

```
{
  "subject": {
    "description": "A young woman with wavy brown hair wearing glasses and a mauve long-sleeve top.",

      "smiling warmly at the viewer"
